 Union Finance Minister Nirmala Sitamaran today Modi government 2
 0 kaa pehla bajet pesh karne ja rahi hai
 It is being called the budget of 'new India', through which the Modi government can take measures to speed up the sluggish economy
 is bajet par corporate-udyog jagat kii najar to he hi, sabase zyada najar us aam aadmi kii he jo berogari or aamadani na badhane se pareshaan he
 In a few hours, Finance Minister Nirmala Sitamaran will start his budget speech, but it should not be difficult for you to understand, for this, we have brought the budget terminology in easy words
 in shabdon ko samaj len, aapke liye bajet samajhnaa aasaan ho jayega
 1
 tex (kar):sarkaar apane kharchon ko puraa karne ke liye aamadani tex se karti he
 It is a type of compulsory payment that the taxpayer has to pay to the government
 yah tex do prakaar hote hai, pratyaksh kar or apratyaksh kar
 The tax that is directly charged to you, such as income tax, corporate tax, tax on income from shares or other assets, property tax, etc
 is called direct tax or direct tax
 duusari taraf, vah tex jise sidhe janata se nahin liya jaataa kintu jiskaa boj aakhirkaar usee par padataa he, use apratyaksh kar kehalaate hai
 For example, excise duty (excise) on goods manufactured in the country, customs duty (custom), service tax, etc
 on goods to be imported or exported are indirect taxes
 2 upkar or adhibhaar (cess evam Surcharge):ses yaa upkar kisi tex ke saath kisi vishesh udyeshy ke liye dhan ikaitha karne ke liye, kar aadhaar (tax base) par hi lagaaya jaataa he
 Such as Clean India Cess, Agricultural Welfare Cess, Clean Environment Cess etc
 adhibhaar yaa sarcharge kar ke upar lagane vaala kar he jisaki gananaa kar daayitv ke aadhaar par kii jaati he
 It is usually applied above the income tax
 3
 Income tax: It depends on our sources of income such as income, investment and interest on it
 4
 Corporate tax (corporate tax): Corporate tax is levied on corporate institutions or firms through which the government makes income
 5
 Excise duties: The tax levied on all products made within the border of the country is called excise duty
 excise duty ko ab jiesti main shaamil kar liya gaya he
 6
 seemaa shulk (customs duties):seemaa shulk un vastuon par lagata he, jo desh main aayaat kii jaati he yaa phir desh ke baahar niryaat kii jaati he
 7
 vittiya varsh:bharat main vittiya varsh kii shuruyaat ek april se hoti he or yah agle saal ke 31 march tak chalata he
 This year's budget will be for the financial year 2019-20 which will be from April 1, 2019 to March 31, 2020
 aisi maang uthati rahi he ki vittiya varsh ko janvari se disambar tak kiya jaae, lekin abhi ise mana nahin gaya he
 8
 short turm or long turm gen:share bazaar main koi bhi vyakti yadi ek saal se kam samay ke liye paise laga kar laabh kamata he to use alpakaalik puunjigat laabh (short-turm capital gen) kehete hai
 The money held in shares for more than a year is called long-term capital gains
 pehle long turm capital gen par tex nahin dene kaa praavdhaan tha lekin 2018-19 ke bajet main is par 10 fisadi tex kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya
 However, this tax has to be paid only on the earning of more than Rs 1 lakh
 9
 Subsidies: To remove economic inequality, the economic benefit given by the government to the common people is called subsidy
 jaise alpiji silinder ke gas bharaane vaale garibon ko sarkaar sabsidi dekar use sasta kar detii he
 It can also be cash, but now most of the subsidy is directly transferred to the beneficiary's account by DBT
 companiyon ko sabsidi tex chhot ke taur par di jaati he taaki audyogic gatividhiyaan badhen or rojgaar paidaa ho
 10
 rajkoshiya niti (fiscal Policy) or rajkoshiya ghaataa (fiscal deficit):yah ek aisi niti hoti he ki jo ki sarkaar kii aay, saarvajanik vyay (raksha, swasthya, shiksha, bijli, sadak aadi), tex kii daron (pratyaksh or apratyaksh), saarvajanik rin, ghate kii vitt vyavastha se sambandhit hoti he
 When expenditure is more than the total annual income of the government, it is called fiscal deficit
 chunki bajtary ghaataa sahi tareeke se sarkaar ke rin dayitvon kii jaankaree nahi detaa he, isliye rajkoshiya ghate kii vyavastha laai gai
 It is also called a financial deficit by some people
 11
 Budgetary deficit: The state of budget deficit arises when the expenses exceed the revenue
 isamen sarkaar kii karj dendaree shaamil nahin hoti
 Budgetary deficit = Total receipts - Total expenditure
 12
 Gross Domestic Product (GDP): GDP is the total sum of total goods and services produced within a country's boundary in a financial year
 ise ek tarah se puri arthvyavastha kaa aakaar maanate hai or isamen badhat kii dar ko hi arthvyavastha kii tarakkee kii dar maani jaati he
 India's GDP growth rate in the last financial year
6
 8 fisadi rahi
 13
 samekit kosh (consolidated Fund):yah bharat sarkaar kaa vah kosh he jisame sarkaar kii samast rajasav praptiyaan, sarkaar dwaara jari kiye gaye trevori bills or vasule gaye rin aadi ko shaamil kiya jaataa hai 
 14
 aakasmik kosh (contingency Fund):is fund main aakasmik vyay ko puraa karne ke liye ek raashi rakhi jaati he
 The expenditure is incurred on such issues which cannot be avoided but later, after taking permission from the Parliament, the money is collected from the accumulated fund and put into it
 is fund par rajyon main rajyapal or centre ke sambandh main raashtrapati kaa adhikaar rahata he
 15
 rajasav praptiyaan (revenue Receipts):aisi praptiyaan jinke lautaane kaa daayitv sarkaar kaa nahi ho yaa jinke saath kisi sampatti kii bikri nahi judi hon, rajasav praptiyaan kehalaati hai
 Due to these receipts, there is no increase in the liability of the government
 inako kar rajasav (inakam tex, corporate tex, jiesti ityadi) or gaiyr-kar rajasav (byaaj, fees, labhaansh) main baanta ja saktaa he
 16
 puunjigat praptiyaan (capital Receipts):aisi saarvajanik praptiyon ko puunjigat praati kehete hai jinase sarkaar ke dendaree main badhat hoti he or sarkaar kii parisampattiyon main kami hoti he
 Such as loans taken from within the country, loans from abroad, loans from the Reserve Bank, etc
 17 
 Revenue Expenditure: Those expenses are kept inside it which neither increases the production capacity of the government nor generates additional income for the future
 Examples: expenditure incurred in running government departments, government subsidy, interest payments on loans, grants to state governments, etc
 18
 puunjigat vyay (capital Expenditure):sarkaar ke un kharchon ko puunjigat vyay ke antargat rakhaa jaataa he jisase sarkaar kii sampattiyon main badhat hoti he, jaise sadak, skool, aspataal, kisi puraane bhawan kii marammat aadi
 19
 yojanagat vyay (planned Expenditure):us vyay ko yojanagat vyay kaha jaataa he jisase utpaadan parisampatti (production assets) kaa nirmaan hota he
 This expenditure is related to various economic welfare schemes, such as construction of schools, roads, hospitals, etc
 20
 non-plan Expenditure: a public expenditure that does not incur any development is counted as a non-plan expenditure
 jaise raksha vyay, pension, mahangaai bhatta, baadh, sookhaa, ola vrishti aadi par kiya gaya kharch aadi
 Funds for this are arranged from the Consolidated Fund of India
